(Working in progress with Marc Bezem)

We want to formalise in HoTT the intuition behind a correspondance between the
concept of *path-over* and its respective *total space*.

% - That the pathover has its own (certain paths in the total space). --TODO

The term *pathover* was briefly mentioned in {% cite hottbook %} and they were
later defined in {% cite Licata2015%} as a dependent path.
The concept is extensivily used in {%cite hott-in:agda %}.

% (in words) about the transport and the notation in the book -- TODO
% which is shorthand for ... using transport function for the definition.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/pathovers-total-space.png)

Let's review first an equality type that is closely related with these PathOvers.
(See also {% cite Licata2015 %} for some extra comments).

{: .foldable}

## Homogeneous equality

The *homogeneous equality* is a type `Path` that relates two elements `a₀` and
`a₁` whose types are *definitionally/judgementally* equal. We denote this type as `Path
{A} a₀ a₁`. The curly braces in Agda stand for *implicit arguments*.
We also use the symbol (`_==_`) to denote this type.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1422" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="1428" class="Number">30</a> <a id="1431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>

## Heterogeneous equality

The heterogeneous equality  in {% cite Licata2015 %} relates two elements
of two different types along an equality α between the types mentioned.
This kind of equality can be formalised as follows in Agda:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1780" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="HEq₁"></a><a id="1785" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1785" class="Datatype">HEq₁</a> <a id="1790" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1791" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1791" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1792" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1794" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1795" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1797" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1799" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1804" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1791" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1805" class="Symbol">)</a>
       <a id="1814" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1816" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1817" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1817" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1819" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1821" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1791" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1827" class="Symbol">)</a>
       <a id="1836" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1839" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1839" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="1841" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="1848" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1817" class="Bound">B</a><a id="1849" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1852" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="1854" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1856" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a><a id="1857" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1859" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1860" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1860" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="1862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1864" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1817" class="Bound">B</a><a id="1865" class="Symbol">)</a>
       <a id="1874" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1876" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1881" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1791" class="Bound">ℓ</a> <a id="1883" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="HEq₁.idp"></a><a id="1891" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1891" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="1895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1897" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="1899" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1900" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1900" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="1902" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1904" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a><a id="1905" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1785" class="Datatype">HEq₁</a> <a id="1914" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1916" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1795" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1918" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="1922" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1900" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="1924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1900" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{% comment %}
> In {%cite McBride2004 %} the author introduced a *heterogeneous equality*, which is an equality type
> `a:A= b:B` that relates two elements `a:A` and `b:B` which may have two judgementally
> distinct types, though the reflexivity constructor applies only when both the
> two types and the two terms are judgementally equal.


> However, McBride’s heterogeneous equality is **logically equivalent** to a
> homogeneous equality type *satisfying uniqueness of identity proofs*, which
> is undesirable **in homotopy type theory, because not all types should be sets**.
{% endcomment %}

We adopt the same name `idp` for the reflexivity constructor of the `Path` type
for the heterogeneous equality. This name is convenient because we want to
maintain some consistency in the following proofs. We will switch between
different definitions of heterogeneous equality but also between definitions for
the homogeneous equality.

Let us recall the transport function and the coercion function  along a
homogeneous equality.

  <a id="10196" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="10203" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10203" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="10212" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10213" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="10216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10216" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10218" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10220" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10221" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10221" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10230" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10213" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="10232" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10235" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="10237" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10221" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10241" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10248" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10216" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10250" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10252" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="10262" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
    <a id="10342" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
    <a id="hott.Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="10384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10384" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="10393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10396" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10398" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10400" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10402" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10404" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10406" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10221" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10409" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10411" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10235" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="10415" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10404" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10416" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10419" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10213" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="10430" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10432" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10216" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10434" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="10440" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10384" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="10449" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10449" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10451" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10451" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10453" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10456" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10456" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10460" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10221" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10461" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10463" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10465" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10449" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10456" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="10472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10451" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#10456" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="11982" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Contractible"></a><a id="11989" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#11989" class="Module">Contractible</a> <a id="12002" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="12013" class="Comment">-- Contractible types. A contractible type is a type such that every</a>
    <a id="12086" class="Comment">-- element is equal to a center of contraction.</a>
    <a id="hott.Contractible.isContr"></a><a id="12138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12138" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="12146" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12148" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="12150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12150" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="12151" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="12154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12155" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="12164" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12150" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="12165" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12167" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12169" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="12174" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12150" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
    <a id="12180" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12138" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="12188" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12188" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12190" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3432" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="12194" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12188" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12196" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="12199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12199" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="12201" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12203" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="12205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12205" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12188" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12212" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12199" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="12216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="12219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12205" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12220" class="Symbol">))</a>

    <a id="12283" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="12290" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12290" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="12314" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12315" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="12318" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12318" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="12320" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12322" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12323" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12325" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="12332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12315" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="12334" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12336" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12337" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="12339" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12341" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="12346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12318" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="12348" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12350" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="12362" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
      <a id="12432" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
      <a id="12499" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
      <a id="hott.Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="12518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12518" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="12529" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12532" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="12534" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12536" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12323" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12538" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12540" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12337" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12541" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12545" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="12550" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12551" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12315" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="12554" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="12556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12318" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="12558" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="13962" class="Comment">-- Application of an homotopy</a>
    <a id="hott.FunctionExtensionality.happly"></a><a id="13996" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function">happly</a> <a id="14003" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13931" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14007" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14014" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14016" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14018" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14020" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13899" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14021" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14023" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13931" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14027" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14016" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14032" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14034" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14016" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14035" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="14041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function">happly</a> <a id="14048" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="14052" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14052" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14054" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14056" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

    <a id="14065" class="Comment">-- The axiom of function extensionality postulates that the</a>
    <a id="14129" class="Comment">-- application of homotopies is an equivalence.</a>
    <a id="14181" class="Keyword">postulate</a> <a id="hott.FunctionExtensionality.axiomFunExt"></a><a id="14191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14191" class="Postulate">axiomFunExt</a> <a id="14203" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12734" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="14213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function">happly</a>

    <a id="hott.FunctionExtensionality.eqFunExt"></a><a id="14225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">eqFunExt</a> <a id="14234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14236" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14237" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13931" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14242" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">g</a><a id="14243" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12874" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="14247" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14249" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13899" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14254" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14258" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13931" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14260" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14249" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14265" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14267" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14249" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14268" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="14274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">eqFunExt</a> <a id="14283" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#13996" class="Function">happly</a> <a id="14292" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14294" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14191" class="Postulate">axiomFunExt</a>

    <a id="14311" class="Comment">-- From this, the usual notion of function extensionality follows.</a>

  <a id="16872" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="16879" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#16879" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="16892" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="16903" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
    <a id="16974" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>

  <a id="28743" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#27454" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a> <a id="28771" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="28779" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28784" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Module">hott</a> <a id="28789" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Let be `α : A == B`, `a : A`, and `b : B` then the following types are equivalent
to the previous type `HEq₁`.

### Equivalences

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29498" class="Comment">-- A proof that HEq₁-≃-HEq₂</a>

Finally, we complete the chain of equivalence with `HEq₄-≃-HEq₁`.

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="32162" class="Comment">-- A proof that HEq₄-to-HEq₁</a>

For the follwing discussion, we may use heterogeneous using the first definition.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="HEq"></a><a id="33093" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#33093" class="Function">HEq</a> <a id="33097" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33099" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1785" class="Datatype">HEq₁</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Path over a path

Given a type family $$C: A → Type$$ and a path $$α : a₁ = a₂$$, a *pathover* is a
path connecting $$c₁ : C a₁$$ with  $$c₂ : C a₂$$  lying over $$α$$.
types.

% -- TODO
The geometry intuition is a path (x,u)= (y,v) which projects down on to p0
them ΣAC is the total space and "projecting down" means ap proj q = p with proj : ΣAC

% --TODO
The geometry intuition has been formalised by {% cite Licata2015 %}
in five different ways as follows.

% The PathOver is the dependent version of a *path*, what it means that the path
% is between two endpoints from maybe different types. This is of course what we
% saw in the definition of the heterogeneous equality. The difference is that
% we simplify `HEq`  definition with `PathOver` by factorizing the type family
% that is involved in the paths.
%
% We define `PathOver₁` as the inductive family with only one constructor,
% the reflexivity over the reflexivity on the base space `A`. To eliminate this
% type, we can use path-over induction. In Agda, we just do pattern matching along
% the path on the base `A`. Additionaly, we can define this notion of PathOvers in at least
% four different ways. Let us see these definitions, all equivalent. To refer to a pathover,
% we adopt the notation `c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ]` from the HoTT-Agda library.

A more direct formalisation is the type

Notice that above when we used `transport C α c₁`, we could also have used `coe (ap C α)`,
we mention this because in HoTT-Agda library, it's defined `transport` using `coe`.

      <a id="39113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#39113" class="Function">PathOver₄~PathOver₃</a> <a id="39133" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#39136" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="39138" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34927" class="Function">PathOver₃</a> <a id="39150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#38204" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="39152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="39156" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#38804" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="39159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#38808" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="39161" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="39173" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39175" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#38432" class="Function">PathOver₄-to-PathOver₃</a> <a id="39198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#38229" class="Function">PathOver₃-to-PathOver₄</a> <a id="39222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#39136" class="Bound">p</a><a id="39223" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="39228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#39136" class="Bound">p</a>
      <a id="39236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#39113" class="Function">PathOver₄~PathOver₃</a> <a id="39256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="39260" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="39305" class="Comment">-- PathOver₄-≃-PathOver₅</a>
<a id="39330" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39333" class="Comment">-- module _ {ℓ} (A : Type ℓ) (C : A → Type ℓ) where</a>
<a id="39385" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39388" class="Comment">--   PathOver₄-to-PathOver₅ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="39468" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₄ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="39502" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="39536" class="Comment">--   PathOver₄-to-PathOver₅ {a₁} {.a₁} {idp} {c₁} {.c₁} idp = idp</a>
<a id="39602" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39605" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-to-PathOver₄ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="39685" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="39719" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₄ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="39753" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-to-PathOver₄ {a₁} {.a₁} {idp} {c₁} {.c₁} idp = idp</a>
<a id="39819" class="Comment">--   --</a>
<a id="39827" class="Comment">--   PathOver₄-≃-PathOver₅ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="39906" class="Comment">--         → PathOver₄ C α c₁ c₂ ≃ PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="39961" class="Comment">--   PathOver₄-≃-PathOver₅ {a₁}{.a₁}{idp}{c₁}{c₂} =</a>
<a id="40013" class="Comment">--     qinv-≃</a>
<a id="40027" class="Comment">--       PathOver₄-to-PathOver₅</a>
<a id="40059" class="Comment">--       (PathOver₅-to-PathOver₄</a>
<a id="40092" class="Comment">--         , PathOver₄~PathOver₅ , PathOver₅~PathOver₄)</a>
<a id="40148" class="Comment">--     where</a>
<a id="40161" class="Comment">--       PathOver₄~PathOver₅ : (p : PathOver₅ C idp c₁ c₂)</a>
<a id="40220" class="Comment">--           → PathOver₄-to-PathOver₅ (PathOver₅-to-PathOver₄ p) == p</a>
<a id="40290" class="Comment">--       PathOver₄~PathOver₅ idp = idp</a>
<a id="40329" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40332" class="Comment">--       PathOver₅~PathOver₄ : (p : PathOver₄ C idp c₁ c₂)</a>
<a id="40391" class="Comment">--           → PathOver₅-to-PathOver₄ (PathOver₄-to-PathOver₅ p) == p</a>
<a id="40461" class="Comment">--       PathOver₅~PathOver₄ idp = idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="40539" class="Comment">-- PathOver₅-≃-PathOver₁</a>
<a id="40564" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40567" class="Comment">-- module _ {ℓ} (A : Type ℓ) (C : A → Type ℓ) where</a>
<a id="40619" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40622" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="40702" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="40736" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₁ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="40770" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁ {a₁} {.a₁} {idp} {c₁} {.c₁} idp = idp</a>
<a id="40836" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="40839" class="Comment">--   PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="40919" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₁ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="40953" class="Comment">--          → PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="40987" class="Comment">--   PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅ {a₁} {.a₁} {idp} {c₁} {.c₁} idp = idp</a>
<a id="41053" class="Comment">--   --</a>
<a id="41061" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-≃-PathOver₁ : {a₁ a₂ : A} {α : a₁ == a₂} {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂}</a>
<a id="41140" class="Comment">--         → PathOver₅ C α c₁ c₂ ≃ PathOver₁ C α c₁ c₂</a>
<a id="41195" class="Comment">--   PathOver₅-≃-PathOver₁ {a₁}{.a₁}{idp}{c₁}{c₂} =</a>
<a id="41247" class="Comment">--     qinv-≃</a>
<a id="41261" class="Comment">--       PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁</a>
<a id="41293" class="Comment">--       (PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅</a>
<a id="41326" class="Comment">--         , PathOver₅~PathOver₁ , PathOver₁~PathOver₅)</a>
<a id="41382" class="Comment">--     where</a>
<a id="41395" class="Comment">--       PathOver₅~PathOver₁ : (p : PathOver₁ C idp c₁ c₂)</a>
<a id="41454" class="Comment">--           → PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁ (PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅ p) == p</a>
<a id="41524" class="Comment">--       PathOver₅~PathOver₁ idp = idp</a>
<a id="41563" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="41566" class="Comment">--       PathOver₁~PathOver₅ : (p : PathOver₅ C idp c₁ c₂)</a>
<a id="41625" class="Comment">--           → PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅ (PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁ p) == p</a>
<a id="41695" class="Comment">--       PathOver₁~PathOver₅ idp = idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prefer the third definition for pathovers that comes from the HoTT book, that is,
PathOver defined by an inductive family. Nevertheless, in the following definition,
the reader can change the subindex of the `PathOver` word to use any other definition.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="42016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="42025" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="42027" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34493" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a>

<a id="42038" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="42044" class="Number">30</a> <a id="42047" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="42056" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="42063" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">PathOver</a> C α c₁ c₂ <a id="42082" class="Symbol">=</a> c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ]{% endraw %}</pre>

> While we have motivated PathOver as a factored heterogeneous equality, there
> is also a geometric intuition. **Dependent types correspond to fibrations**, so a
> type `C : A → Type` can be pictured as its total space `∑ a:A . C` a projecting
> down to `A` by first projection.

> A **path-over** `γ : PathOver C α c­₁ c₂` represents a path σ in `∑ a:A . C` a
> a between `(a₁, c₁)` and `(a₂,c₂)`, such that ap fst σ is exactly `α`. That
> is, it is a path in the total space that projects down to, or lies over, `α`
> (path pairing `pair= α γ` will be made precise below).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="42706" class="Comment">-- An extra and useful function:</a>
<a id="42739" class="Comment">-- to make dependent pairs</a>

  <a id="42856" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42858" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42859" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42859" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="42861" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42819" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="42866" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="42869" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42822" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="42871" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="42875" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42878" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42878" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="42880" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42882" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42831" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="42885" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">==</a> <a id="42888" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42843" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="42891" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">[</a> <a id="42893" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42799" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="42895" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="42897" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42859" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="42899" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">]</a><a id="42900" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="42905" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42908" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42819" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="42911" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="42913" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42831" class="Bound">c₁</a><a id="42915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="42917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="42920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42822" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="42924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="42926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42843" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="42928" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="42930" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42766" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="42936" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="42940" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="42944" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="42946" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4426" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="42949" class="Symbol">(_</a> <a id="42952" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,_</a><a id="42954" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="42956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Total spaces

We want to prove the following lemma:

**Lemma.** Let be `A : Type` and `C : A → Type` with two terms `a₁ a₂ : A` and a
path between them `α : a₁ == a₂`. If  `c₁ : C a₁`, `c₂ : C a₂` then there is an
correspondence between a term in the total space and the pathover between c₁ and c₁
along the path `α`.

<p class="equation">
$$
 \sum\limits_{(a₁ , c₁) = (a₂ , c₂)} \ (\mathsf{ap}~\mathsf{fst}~q~= \alpha)
  \simeq \mathsf{PathOver}~C~α~c₁~c₂.
$$
</p>

To show such a equivalence, we proceed defining the functions back and forth,
the two homotopies associated to these functions with the identity and finally,
we prove the equivalence using the quasiinverse version for the equivalence type.

- Let us define the function `Σ-to-==[↓]` that maps a term of the sigma type to
a pathover. This construction is using Σ-induction followed by two
path-induction on the identity types from the components.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="43902" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="43909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43909" class="Module">_</a> <a id="43911" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43912" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43912" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="43915" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43915" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="43917" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="43919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43919" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="43921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="43928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43912" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="43930" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="43932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="43934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43936" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43919" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="43938" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43940" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="43945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43915" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="43947" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="43949" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="43952" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="43955" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43919" class="Bound">A</a><a id="43958" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43960" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="43991" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="44001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44001" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="44012" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44014" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44015" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44015" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="44017" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44019" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="44022" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="44025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="44027" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="44029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44029" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="44032" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44034" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44036" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="44038" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="44040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44040" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="44043" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44045" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44047" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="44049" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="44055" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44057" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3432" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="44059" class="Symbol">((</a><a class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44070" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="44073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="44077" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="44079" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44040" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="44081" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="44084" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="44087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44087" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="44089" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44091" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44092" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4426" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="44095" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3532" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="44099" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44087" class="Bound">q</a><a id="44100" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="44105" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44015" class="Bound">α</a><a id="44106" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="44112" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44029" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="44117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">==</a> <a id="44120" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44040" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="44123" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">[</a> <a id="44125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44127" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">↓</a>  <a id="44130" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44015" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="44132" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="44136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44001" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="44147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44148" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="44152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="44154" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="44157" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44159" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="44161" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

- The inverse function to the previous one is `==[↓]-to-Σ`, which sends
  pathovers to a dependent pair as it follows. Its construction is by using
  path-induction on `α` in the base space, follows by path-induction on `γ`. The
  goal after this becomes in a pair of two reflexivity proofs `(a₁ , c₁) == (a₁
  , c₁)` and `(a₁ == a₁) == (a₁ == a₁)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="44542" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="44552" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44552" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="44563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44565" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44566" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44566" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="44568" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44570" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="44573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="44576" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="44578" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="44580" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44580" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="44583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44585" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44587" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="44589" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="44591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44591" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="44594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="44600" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="44606" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44608" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44609" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44609" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="44611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44613" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44580" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="44616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">==</a> <a id="44619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44591" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="44622" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">[</a> <a id="44624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="44626" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="44628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44566" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="44630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">]</a><a id="44631" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="44637" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44639" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3432" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="44641" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="44643" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="44646" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4426" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="44677" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44566" class="Bound">α</a><a id="44688" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="44692" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44552" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="44703" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44704" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="44707" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="44713" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="44715" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="44720" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="44722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="44725" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="44730" class="Comment">-- -- more explict:</a>
  <a id="44752" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {idp}{c₁}{c₂} idp = (idp {a = (a₁ , c₁)}, idp {a = idp {a = a₁}})</a>

  <a id="44835" class="Comment">-- -- Alternative way to construct this function is (also type-checked):</a>
  <a id="44910" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {α = α} γ = (pair= α γ , ap-fst-pair= α γ)</a>
  <a id="44969" class="Comment">--   where</a>
  <a id="44982" class="Comment">--</a>
  <a id="44987" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= : (α : a₁ == a₂)</a>
  <a id="45024" class="Comment">--       → {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂} (γ : c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ] )</a>
  <a id="45086" class="Comment">--       → ap fst (pair= α γ) == α</a>
  <a id="45123" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= idp idp = idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The respective homotopies

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="45207" class="Comment">-- Homotopies</a>
  <a id="45223" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45223" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]∘==[↓]-to-Σ∼id</a>
    <a id="45252" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="45254" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45255" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="45257" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="45259" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="45262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="45265" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="45267" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="45269" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45269" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="45272" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="45274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="45276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43949" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="45278" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="45280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45280" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="45283" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="45285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="45287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43952" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="45289" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="45295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="45297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45298" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="45300" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="45302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45269" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="45305" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">==</a> <a id="45308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45280" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="45311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">[</a> <a id="45313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#43932" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="45315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="45317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45255" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="45319" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#42016" class="Function">]</a><a id="45320" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="45326" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="45328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44001" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="45339" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45340" class="Argument">α</a> <a id="45342" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45344" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45255" class="Bound">α</a><a id="45345" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="45347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#44552" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="45359" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45298" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="45360" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="45362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="45365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45298" class="Bound">γ</a>
  <a id="45369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45223" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]∘==[↓]-to-Σ∼id</a> <a id="45394" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45395" class="Argument">α</a> <a id="45397" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="45402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="45404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="45408" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1495" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

  <a id="45417" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#45417" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ∘Σ-to-==[↓]∼id</a>

Finally, we show the equivalence using the fact above proved.

## Other facts

We can build a dependent path by applying a depedent function to a homogeneous path.

## Extra

- **Lemma 1**. If $$A: U$$ and $$P: A → U$$ and $$f: A' \simeq A$$, then
$$\sum_A P \simeq \sum_{A'} (P ∘ f)$$.

- **Lemma 2.** If $$A: U$$ and $$P: A → U$$ and $$a: A$$,
then $$\sum_{(w:\sum_{A} P)}  \(\mathsf{fst } w = a) \simeq Pa$$

The previous fact can also seen as a case of the following lemma.
If `A : Type` and `C : A → Type`, we can show that:

          <a id="47382" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="47384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46772" class="Function">l→</a> <a id="47387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47312" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47131" class="Function">l←</a> <a id="47393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47312" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47336" class="Bound">pΣbP&#39;</a><a id="47400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="47402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="47405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47336" class="Bound">pΣbP&#39;</a>
  <a id="47413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47272" class="Function">l→∘l←-~-id</a> <a id="47424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47425" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47425" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="47427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47429" class="Bound">eqf</a><a id="47432" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="47434" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47435" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="47437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47439" class="Bound">p</a><a id="47440" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="47442" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="47448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#15829" class="Function">Σ-bycomponents</a>
      <a id="47469" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="47471" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4877" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
            <a id="47489" class="Symbol">{!   !}</a>
        <a id="47505" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4706" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="47509" class="Symbol">{!   !}</a> <a id="47517" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4706" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="47529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47435" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="47532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4811" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="47533" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="47536" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47538" class="Symbol">{!   !})</a>

  <a id="47554" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47554" class="Function">l←∘l→-~-id</a> <a id="47565" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47567" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47568" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="47570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47572" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1033" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="47577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46724" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="47579" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="47591" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="47593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47594" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47568" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="47600" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#12874" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="47602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46733" class="Bound">A</a><a id="47603" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="47615" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="47617" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47618" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47618" class="Bound">pΣaP</a> <a id="47623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="47625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3432" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="47627" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46733" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="47629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46746" class="Bound">P</a><a id="47630" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="47642" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="47644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47131" class="Function">l←</a> <a id="47647" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47594" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47650" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#46772" class="Function">l→</a> <a id="47653" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47594" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47618" class="Bound">pΣaP</a><a id="47659" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="47661" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1441" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="47664" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47618" class="Bound">pΣaP</a>
  <a id="47671" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47554" class="Function">l←∘l→-~-id</a> <a id="47682" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47682" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="47684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="47685" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47685" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="47687" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47689" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#47689" class="Bound">p</a><a id="47690" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="47692" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="47694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#15829" class="Function">Σ-bycomponents</a> <a id="47709" class="Symbol">({!   !}</a> <a id="47718" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47720" class="Symbol">{!   !})</a>
  <a id="47731" class="Comment">--</a>
  <a id="47736" class="Comment">--</a>
  <a id="47741" class="Comment">-- lemma : {B : Type ℓᵢ} → (e : B ≃ A) → Σ A P ≃ Σ B (λ b → P ((fst e) b))</a>
  <a id="47818" class="Comment">-- lemma {B} e = qinv-≃ (l→ e) (l← e , l→∘l←-~-id e , {!   !})</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Using Univalence axiom:

{: .foldable}
